 madhavan nair ke kaarykaal main isro ne chandramaa par chandrayan mishan launch kiya tha

 bataa den ki isro ne 15 farvari ko videshi graahakon ke liye ek rakam lekar antariksh main 100 se adhik naino or micro upgrah chode the

 Nair said, "these nano satellites, which leave debris after a short stay in space, can become a threat to us

 " purv isro adhyaksh ne chetavanee bhare lahaze main kaha ki isro ko 500 kilometre kii kaksha main videshi naino upgrahon kii lonching se hone vaale kuch lakh dollar ke laabh ko, vartmaan or bhavishya main unke margo ke kareeb sthapit bhu-avlokan upgrahon ko hone vaale sambhavit khatre se naap-tol kar dekhnaa chahie
 He also said that India will have to compensate in the event of the debris of any of these nano satellites and the collision with the active satellite of another country in the future
 nair 'antariksh daayitv sankalp' kaa zikr kar rahe the, jo 1972 main prabhavi hua tha
 Under this, the countries leaving the satellite will have to "take international responsibility for the satellites released from their territory, irrespective of the country

 Let us tell you that on February 15, ISRO left more than 100 nano and micro satellites in space, taking an amount for foreign customers
 inamen se 'dovs' naamak 88 upgrah san francisco kii ek start-ap 'planet' ke hai

 nair ne kaha, "main thodaa chintit hum, kyonki jis sthaan par inhen sthapit kiya gaya he, yah vahi sthaan he, jahaan hamaare bhu-avlokan upgrah hai yaa honge
 " nair ne kaha ki naino upgrahon kaa upyogi jivan behad kam hota he, jiske baad ve kachra ban jate hai or antariksh main usee kaksha main ghoomte rahete hai

 Putrada Ekadashi has special significance in Hinduism
 hindu panchang ke mutabik, saal main 24 ekadashiyaan padati hai, jinamein se do ko putrada ekadshi ke naam se janaa jaataa he
 Putrada Ekadashi falls in Shravan and Pausha Shukla Paksha
 donon hi ekadashiyon kaa vishesh mahatv he
 It is believed that the effects of this fast give children
 aapako bataa den ki hindu panchang kii 11veen tithi ko ekadshi (ekadashi) kehete hai
 This date comes twice in a month
 poornima ke baad or amavasya ke baad

 NPCI is currently offering rupay Debit Card

 Explain that till now Rupay is an ATM card based on India's indigenous payment system
 ise vija or master card kii tarah prayog kiya jaataa he
 The rupay card was developed by NPCI in April 2011

 What are the Akharas? In Kumbh, the Akharas have special importance
 akhaade shabd kii shuruyaat mughalkaal ke daur se hui
 The arena is that group of sadhus who also excel in armaments
 kya hoti he peshwai?jab kumbh main naachte-gaate dhoomdhaam se akhaade jate hai, to use peshwai kehete hai
 Shankaracharya is said to have built 13 akharas in the eighth century
 tab se vahi akhaade bane hue the
 But this time another arena has been added, due to which, this time, you will get to see the presence of 14 akharas in Kumbh
 aaie jaane in 14 akhaadon ke bare main
 
 
 1
 atal akhaada-inke isht dev bhagwaan ganesh hai
 Only Brahmins, Kshatriyas and Vaishyas can take initiation in this arena and no other can enter this arena
 yah sabase pracheen akhaadon main se ek mana jaataa he
 2
 avaahan akhaada-inke isht dev shri dattatreya or shri gajanan dono hai
 The center of this arena is Kashi
 3
 Niranjani Arena - This arena is the most educated arena
 is akhaade main kareeb 50 mahamandaleshrchar hai
 His Ishta Dev is Kartik, son of Lord Shankar
 is akhaade kii sthapana 826 isvi main hui thi
 4
 panchagni akhaada-is akhaade main keval brahmacharee brahman hi diksha le sakate he
 His presiding deity is Gayatri and his main center is Kashi
 5
 The responsibility of worshiping the Mahanirvana Arena - Mahakaleshwar Jyotirlinga is with this arena
 inke isht dev kapil mahamuni hai
 They were founded in 671 AD
 6
 Anand Arena - This arena was established in 855 AD
 is akhaade ke acharya kaa pad hi pramukh hota he
 Its center is Varanasi
 7
 Of the three Ani Akharas of the Nirmohi akhara-vaishnava sect, this includes the largest number of akharas
 is akhaade kii sthapana ramanandacharya ne 1720 main kii thi
 The temples of this arena are located in places like Uttar Pradesh, Madhya Pradesh, Gujarat, Bihar, Rajasthan etc
 8
 Big nostalgic Panchayati Arena - This arena started in 1910
 is akhaade ke sansthaapak shrichandraacharya udasin hai
 The objective of this arena is to serve
 9
 New Indifferent Arena - This arena started in 1710
 manyata he ki is akhaade ko bada udasin akhaade ke saadhuon ne banaaya tha
 10
 nirmal akhaada-is akhaade kii sthapana shridurgasingh maharaj ne kii thi, jinke ishtdev pustak shri gurugranth sahib hai
 It is said that the people of this arena are not allowed to smoke like other arenas
 11
 Vaishnava Arena - This arena was founded by Madhyamurari
 12
 Nagapanti Gorakhnath Arena - This arena was established in 866 AD, the founder of which is Pir Shivnathji
 13
 Juna Akhara - This arena is Kishtadevarudravatar Dattatreya
 haridwar main is akhaade kaa ashram he
 The Peethadheeshwara Swami Awadheshanand Giri Maharaj of this arena is
 14
 Kinnar Arena - Till now, Kumbh Arena had to offer 13 Akharas, but this time Kinnar Arena has also been included in Kumbh

 jo ki nindaneey he
